 17     Program was assigning your current account(s) to Republic Bank.
 18

 5      As you know, Deaconess Health System, Inc. has arranged with Republic Bank & Trust Company ("Republic Bank") and EPI
 6      Finance Group, LLC, to offer the Extended Payments without Interest (EPI) Progam which allows you to receive a 0%
 7      Annual Percentage Rate ("APR"), interest-free loan to pay your health care account(s).  Because you have incurred
 8      additional charges at Deaconess Health System, Inc., you can now amend your existing EPI loan account and pay your
 9      new account balance over time.
 10      
 11     Republic Bank has reviewed your EPI loan application and has approved you for the following amended terms:
 12      
 13     Loan Terms: <<RTEBAL>>
 14     Monthly Payment: <<DSMINPAY>>
 15     Loan Term: <<DU10004>>
 16     APR: 0%
 17     Interest Rate: 0%
 18

 20     forth above:
 21

 24      
 25     See Notes 1 and 2 below for an explanation of when these fees may be added to a particular monthly
 26     payment.

 32     located on the enclosed monthly billing statement.
 33      
 34     1  If we do not receive your payment of the full monthly payment amount by 5:00 p.m. Eastern Standard
 35        Time on the date that is seven days after the date it is due, we will consider it late and will
 36        charge you $25.  This fee will be included on your next monthly billing statement.
 37      
 38     2  We will charge you a $20 Returned Check Fee if your check, ACH payment, or other electronic
 39        payment is returned to us because you have insufficient funds in your account to cover such
 40        payment.  This fee will be included on your next monthly billing statement.
 41      
 42     By making your first payment, you agree to pay Republic Bank in accordance with terms of this
 43     Patient Terms and Agreement.  If at any time, you are 67 days past due on your account (either
 44     consecutive or nonconsecutive missed payments), we will consider you to be in default and this
 45     Patient Terms and Agreement will be terminated.

 47     Please note: You are always permitted to pay the outstanding balance in full with no
 48     prepayment penalty.
 49      
 50     If you do not want to participate in the EPI Program, you may make arrangements to pay your
 51     account balance in full directly to Deaconess Health System, Inc. by calling 800.467.6802.

 1      FACTS
 2      WHAT DOES REPUBLIC CREDIT SOLUTIONS, A DIVISION OF REPUBLIC BANK & TRUST
 3      COMPANY, DO WITH YOUR PERSONAL INFORMATION?
 4       
 5      Why?
 6      Financial companies choose how they share your personal information.
 7      Federal law gives consumers the right to limit some but not all sharing.
 8      Federal law also requires us to tell you how we collect, share, and
 9      protect your personal information. Please read this notice carefully to
 10     understand what we do.
 11      
 12     What?
 13     The types of personal information we collect and share depend on the
 14     product or service you have with us. This information can include:
 15          Social Security number and payment history
 16          transaction history and credit history
 17          credit card or other debt and employment information
 18     When you are no longer our customer, we continue to share information as
 19     described in this notice.
 20      
 21     How?
 22     All financial companies need to share customers personal information to
 23     run their everyday business. In the section below, we list all the
 24     reasons financial companies can share their customers information; the
 25     reasons Republic Credit Solutions, a division of Republic Bank & Trust
 26     Company chooses to share; and whether you can limit this sharing.
 27      
 28     Reasons we can share your personal information
 29     Does Republic Credit Solutions, a division of Republic Bank & Trust
 30     Company share?
 31     Can you limit this sharing?
 32      
 33     For our everyday business - such as to process your transaction, maintain
 34     your account(s), respond to court orders and legal investigations, or
 35     report to credit bureaus
 36     Yes                                    No
 37      
 38     For our marketing purposes - To offer our products and services to you
 39     Yes                                    No
 40      
 41     For joint marketing with other financial companies
 42     Yes                                    No
 43      
 44     For our affiliates' everyday business purposes - information about your
 45     transactions and experiences
 46     Yes                                    No
 47      
 48     For our affiliates' everyday business purpose - information about your
 49     creditworthiness
 50     No                                     We don't share
 51      
 52     For nonaffiliates to market you
 53     No                                     We don't share
 54

 1      FACTS
 2      WHAT DOES REPUBLIC CREDIT SOLUTIONS, A DIVISION OF REPUBLIC BANK & TRUST
 3      COMPANY, DO WITH YOUR PERSONAL INFORMATION?
 4       
 5      Why?
 6      Financial companies choose how they share your personal information.
 7      Federal law gives consumers the right to limit some but not all sharing.
 8      Federal law also requires us to tell you how we collect, share, and
 9      protect your personal information. Please read this notice carefully to
 10     understand what we do.
 11      
 12     What?
 13     The types of personal information we collect and share depend on the
 14     product or service you have with us. This information can include:
 15          Social Security number and payment history
 16          transaction history and credit history
 17          credit card or other debt and employment information
 18     When you are no longer our customer, we continue to share information as
 19     described in this notice.
 20

 23     run their everyday business. In the section below, we list all the
 24     reasons financial companies can share their customers information; the
 25     reasons Republic Credit Solutions, a division of Republic Bank & Trust
